🔬 2. Hojiwwan Ijoo (Key Activities) Jahan AFOLU Itoophiyaa

AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara Bineensota Bosonaa fi Tuuriizimii keessatti hojiiwwan ijoo jaha (6) irratti xiyyeeffata. Hojiiwwan kunneen qindoominaan kan hojjetaman yoo ta'u, eegumsa lubbu-qabeenyaa irraa kaasee hanga misooma tuuriizimii uumamaa itti fufiinsa qabuutti, akkasumas hordoffii bineensotaa irraa kaasee hanga jireenya hawaasaa fooyyessuutti walitti hidhamanii hojjetamu. Karaa kanaan, AFOLU Itoophiyaan furmaata bal'aa, ragaa qabatamaa irratti hundaa'e fi hawaasa naannoo fayyadu dhiyeessuun, eegumsa lubbu-qabeenya biyyaalessaa fi misooma diinagdee baadiyyaa walumaan dhugoomsa.

01
🏞
Bulchiinsa Naannoo Tikfamaa Cimsu
Protected Area Management Support & Capacity Building

Naannoolee tikfamaan Itoophiyaa keessa jiran, kanneen akka Paarkii Biyyaalessaa Tulluu Baalee, Simien, Sululaa Oomoo, Awaash fi naannoolee biroo, qabeenya lubbu-qabeenya biyyaalessaa keessaa kan ijoo kan ta'aniidha. Naannoolee kanneen hoggansa gahaa, humna namaa leenji'ee fi meeshaalee teeknooloojii ammayyaatiin cimsuun hojii eegumsaa naannoo irratti dhiibbaa olaanaa qaba. AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara kana keessatti ragaa teechnikaa, leenjii ogummaa fi gorsa qabatamaa kennuun, hoggansa naannoolee tikfamaa cimsuun, qabeenyi lubbu-qabeenyaa kun haalaan akka tikfamu gadi fageenyaan hojjeta.

  • Madaallii bu'a-qabeessummaa hoggansaa: madaallii bu'a-qabeessummaa hoggansa naannoolee tikfamaa (Management Effectiveness Tracking Tool (METT)) gaggeessuu fi deeggaruun, eessatti hanqinni jiru adda baasuun fooyya'iinsaaf qajeelfama dhiyeessuu
  • Leenjii eeggdota fi hojjettootaa: eeggdota naannoo tikfamaa (rangers) fi hojjettoota paarkiifi leenjii teeknikaa, akkasumas hordoffii dijitaalaa (digital monitoring) irratti leenjii ogummaa kennuun, dandeettii hojii guyyuu cimsuu
  • Karoora hoggansaa fooyyessuu: Karoora Hoggansa Naannoo Tikfamaa (Management Plans) fooyyessuuf ragaa qorannoo saayinsaawaa fi gorsa qabatamaa dhiyeessuun, karoorri kun haalaan hojiirra akka oolu mirkaneessuu
  • Bulchiinsa naannoo daangaa: naannoolee daangaa paarkii (buffer zones) sirritti bulchuun, hawaasa naannoo fi naannoo tikfamaa gidduutti tokkummaa fi waliigaltee uumuu, kunis tokkoon tokkoon isaanii kan biraa irraa fayyaduu mirkaneessuu
  • Daldala bineensotaa seeraan ala ittisuu: hojii adamoo seeraan alaa (anti-poaching) fi daldala bineensotaa seeraan alaa (illegal wildlife trade) hordofuu fi ittisuu keessatti deeggarsa teeknikaa, ragaa fi gorsa kennuu
  • Walitti hidhamiinsa naannoolee tikfamaa: naannoolee tikfamaa adda addaa gidduutti karaaleen bineensonni walitti dhufanii sosoochaan (wildlife corridors) akka argaman karoorsuu fi deeggaruun, baay'ina jeenii (genetic diversity) fi jiraachisaa lubbu-qabeenyaa eegsisuu
02
⚔
Wal-falmiinsa Bineensaa fi Namaa Furuu
Human-Wildlife Conflict Mitigation Programs

Bineensonni bosonaa horii hawaasaa fixuu, oomisha qonnaa balleessuu, akkasumas yeroo tokko tokko namootatti miidhaa geessisuu, hawaasa naannoo paarkii fi bosona keessa jiraataniif rakkoo guddaa fi yaaddoo guyyuu ta'eera. Kanaaf, hawaasni miidhaa argamu sirritti dhiphata, bineensonnis akka diinaatti waan ilaalamaniif, eegumsa lubbu-qabeenyaa irratti dhiibbaa olaanaa qaba. AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara kana keessatti wal-falmiinsa bineensaa fi namaa hir'isuuf furmaata saayinsaawaa, hawwataa fi hawaasaaf mijatu, bineensotaa fi namootni nagaan akka jiraatan kan taasisu, ni barbaada.

  • Wal-falmiinsa hordofuu fi kaartessuu: hammam akka wal-falmiinsi mudatu hordofuun, naannoolee miidhaan baay'inaan ka'u (hotspot areas) kaartaa irratti agarsiisuun, qaamolee dhimmichi ilaalu hundaaf ragaa qabatamaa dhiyeessuu
  • Sirna akeekkachiisaa hatattamaa: sirna akeekkachiisa hatattamaa (early warning systems), kan bineensonni hawaasatti dhiyaachuu odeeffannoodhaan ibsu, dhaabuun hawaasni dursee akka of qopheessu mijeessuu
  • Ittisa qabatamaa hojiirra oolchuu: ittisa qaamaa, kanneen akka dallaa kanniisaa (beehive fences), dallaa berbere qabatamaa (chili barriers) fi ifa eegumsaa (guardian lights), babal'isuun bineensonni iddoo hawaasaa akka hin seenne ittisuu
  • Sirna beenyaa cimsuu: sirna beenyaa miidhaa bineensaan ka'u (compensation schemes) qaamolee mootummaa fi dhuunfaa waliin ta'uun ijaaruu fi cimsuun, hawaasni miidhamtoota ta'an gargaarsa qabatamaa akka argatan mirkaneessuu
  • Garee hordoffii hawaasaa ijaaruu: garee hordoffii hawaasa irratti hundaa'an (community-based monitoring teams) gurmeessuun, hawaasni mataa isaatii bineensota naannoo isaanii akka hordofu fi to'atu dandeessisuu
  • Leenjii fi hubannoo hawaasaa: hawaasaaf leenjii fi beekumsa, bineensota bosonaa waliin akkamitti nagaan jiraachuu akka danda'an, kennuun, ilaalcha hawaasaa jijjiiruu fi haala wal-jiraachuu uumuu
03
🤝
Naannoo Tikfamaa Hawaasaa Ijaaruu
Community Conservation Area Development

Paarkoota biyyaalessaa alatti, naannoolee hawaasaan mataa isaatiin tiksuu fi bulchu (Community Conservation Areas (CCAs)) Itoophiyaa keessatti bal'inaan jiru. Naannoolee kunneen, hoggansa hawaasaa fi mirga seeraa naannoolee tikfamaa idil-addunyaa (IUCN Category VI) waliin walsiman qabaachuun, eegumsa lubbu-qabeenyaa keessatti gahee guddaa qabu. AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara kana keessatti hawaasni bineensotaa fi qabeenya uumamaa naannoo isaanii tiksuun galii qabatamaa, kan tuuriizimii uumamaa, oomishaalee bosonaa muka-maleeyyii (NTFPs) fi gurgurtaa kaarboonii irraa argamu, akka argatan mirkaneessuuf, CCAs ijaaruu, deeggaruu fi cimsuu irratti hojjeta.

  • CCAs seeraan diriirfachuu: Naannoolee Tikfamaa Hawaasaa qaamolee mootummaa waliin ta'uun seeraan diriirsuu fi galmeessuu, kunis abbummaa fi mirga hawaasaa qabatamaadhaan mirkaneessa
  • Mirga hawaasaa cimsuu: hawaasaaf mirga CCA hoggansuu (governance), galii argamu fayyadamuu (benefit sharing) fi murtii dhalan kennuu (decision-making) seeraan mirkaneessuu
  • Karoora hoggansaa qopheessuu: Karoora Hoggansa CCA (Management Plans) kan hawaasaan mataa isaatiin qopheessu, ragaa saayinsaawaadhaan deeggarame, hojjechiisuu fi qaamolee dhimmichi ilaalu birra raggaasisuu
  • Hordoffii bineensotaa diriirsuu: CCA keessatti bineensota fi lubbu-qabeenya bal'aa hordofuuf sirna ragaa qabatamaa fi hordoffii dijitaalaa dhaabuu, kunis bu'aa hojii eegumsaa madaaluuf bu'uura ta'a
  • Sirna qooddii galii cimsuu: galii CCA irraa, kan tuuriizimii uumamaa fi gurgurtaa kaarboonii (carbon credits) irraa argamu, hawaasaaf qixxummaadhaan akka qoodamu sirna iftoomina qabu diriirsuu fi cimsuu
  • Muuxannoo wal-jijjiiruu: CCA naannoolee milkaa'ina argate adda baasuun, waltajjii muuxannoo wal-jijjiiruu (peer learning platforms) qopheessuun, naannoolee biroo birattis akka babal'atu taasisuu
04
📊
Hordofuu Bineensota fi Madaallii
Wildlife Population Monitoring & Evaluation

Bineensota fi lubbu-qabeenya bal'aa sirritti tiksuuf, jalqaba bineensonni hangam akka jiran, eessatti akka argaman, haala isaanii fi sababii baay'inni isaanii hir'achaa dhufe gadi fageenyaan beekuun murteessaa dha. Gaaffiiwwan kanneen ragaa qabatamaa fi madaallii saayinsaawaadhaan deebii kennuun yoo hin danda'amne, eegumsi hojiirra ooluu dadhaba. AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara kana keessatti sirna hordoffii saayinsaawaa, madaallii qabatamaa fi sassaabbii ragaa fooyya'aa dhaabuu fi cimsuu irratti hojjeta. Karaa kanaan, qaamolee dhimmichi ilaalu hundaaf ragaa amanamaa dhiyeessuun, murtii eegumsaa qajeelaa kennamuu danda'u taasisa.

  • Madaallii baay'ina bineensotaa: madaallii baay'ina bineensotaa, kanneen akka kameeraa kiyyoo (camera traps), tarree sakatta'iinsaa (transect surveys) fi lakkoofsa qilleensa irraa (aerial counts) fayyadamuun gaggeessuu, kunis ragaa qabatamaa baay'ina, gosaa fi gurmuu bineensotaa kenna
  • Hordoffii GPS fayyadamuun: bineensotatti meeshaa GPS/raadiyoo (GPS/radio collaring) hidhuun ragaa sosocho'iinsaa, iddoo jireenyaa fi haala jireenyaa isaanii sirritti hordofuu
  • Saayinsii lammiilee: sagantaa Saayinsii Lammiilee (Citizen Science Programs) qopheessuun, hawaasa naannoo, tuuristoota fi barattoota irraa ragaa sassaabuun, sirna hordoffii bal'aa fi qabatamaa diriirsuu
  • Madaallii ekoolojii yeroo dheeraa: iddoo madaallii ekoolojii yeroo dheeraa (long-term ecological monitoring plots) qopheessuun, jijjiirama yeroo yerootti uumamu hordofuu fi xiinxaluu
  • Madaallii jiraachisaa lubbu-qabeenyaa: madaallii jiraachisaa baay'ina bineensotaa (Population Viability Analysis (PVA)) gaggeessuun, gosti tokko balaa hangam jala akka jiru fi carraan milkaa'inaa hangam akka qabu adda baasuu
  • Gabaasa yeroon qopheessuu: gabaasa hordoffii fi madaallii bineensotaa yeroo isaa eeggatee qopheessuun, qaamolee mootummaa, dhaabbilee idil-addunyaa (CITES, IUCN, CBD) fi qaamolee dhimmichi ilaalu hundaaf dhiyeessuu
05
🏕
Misooma Tuuriizimii Itti Fufiinsa Qabu fi Galii Hawaasaa
Ecotourism Product Development & Community Enterprise

Tuuriizimiin Itoophiyaa galii biyyaalessaaf qabatamaa kan gumaachu yoo ta'u, sadarkaa olaanaa bara 2019tti doolaara biiliyoona 4.8 ga'uun GDP biyyattii cimseera. Haa ta'u malee, hawaasni naannoo paarkii fi bosona keessa jiraatu, kan qabeenya uumamaa fi lubbu-qabeenya tikseef bu'aa argamu keessaa hanga barbaadamu hin argatu. AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara kana keessatti oomishaalee tuuriizimii uumamaa (ecotourism products), kanneen akka simbirroo daawwachuu (birdwatching), saafarii bineensota bosonaa (wildlife safaris) fi tuuriizimii aadaa (cultural tourism), qopheessuu fi babal'isuu irratti hojjeta. Karaa kanaan, hawaasni naannoo qabatamaadhaan galii akka argatuu fi eegumsa lubbu-qabeenyaa irratti hirmaattota qabatamoo akka ta'an mirkaneessa.

  • Oomishaalee tuuriizimii qopheessuu: oomishaalee tuuriizimii uumamaa naannoolee garaa garaaf mijatan, akka simbirroo daawwachuu, daawwannaa bineensota bosonaa, kaaree tulluu fi tuuriizimii aadaa, qopheessuu fi babal'isuu
  • Daldala tuuriizimii hawaasaa ijaaruu: daldala tuuriizimii hawaasa irratti hundaa'an (community-based tourism enterprises), kanneen akka mana keessummaa hawaasaa (lodges), tajaajila qajeelchaa (guiding services) fi oomisha aadaa (handicrafts), ijaaruu fi cimsuu keessatti ogummaan deeggaruu
  • Walitti hidhamiinsa gabaa cimsuu: dhaabbilee tuuriizimii (tour operators) fi tuuristoota walitti fiduun, walitti hidhamiinsa gabaa (market linkage) hawaasa biraan ga'u cimsuun, oomishni hawaasaa salphaatti gabaa akka argatu mirkaneessuu
  • Qajeelchitoota leenjisuu: qajeelchitoota tuuriizimii uumamaa (eco-guides) fi eeggdota hawaasaa (community rangers) leenjisuu, akkasumas mirkaneessaa ogummaa (certification) kennuun, sadarkaa tajaajilaa olaanaa mirkaneessuu
  • Sirna qooddii galii cimsuu: galii tuuriizimii irraa argamu hawaasni qixxummaadhaan akka qooddatu (benefit sharing) sirna iftoomina qabu diriirsuu fi cimsuun, hawaasni eegumsa irraa bu'aa kallattii akka argatu taasisuu
  • Beeksisa tuuriizimii cimsuu: tuuriizimii uumamaa Itoophiyaa sadarkaa biyyaalessaa fi idil-addunyaarratti beeksisuu fi babal'isuuf (marketing and promotion) tarsiimoo qabatamaa hojjechiisuu
06
📘
Ijaarsa Dandeettii fi Beekumsa Walqooddachuu
Capacity Building, Education & Policy Advocacy

Lubbu-qabeenya bal'aa fi bineensota bosonaa Itoophiyaa sirritti tiksuuf, ogeessonni saayinsii lubbu-qabeenyaa, hawaasni naannoo, qaamoleen mootummaa fi qooda-fudhattoonni hundi dandeettii, beekumsa fi muuxannoo gahaa qabaachuu qaban. AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara kana keessatti leenjii ogummaa, qorannoo qabatamaa fi marii imaammataa qindeessuun, akkasumas imaammata bineensota bosonaa fi tuuriizimii uumamaa fooyyessuuf ragaa saayinsaawaa qaamolee imaammata baasaniif dhiyeessuun, gama kanaan riqicha saayinsii fi imaammataa ta'uun hojjeta.

  • Leenjii ogummaa kennuu: ogeessota lubbu-qabeenyaa (wildlife experts), eeggdota naannoo tikfamaa (rangers) fi hojjettoota eegumsa lubbu-qabeenyaa (conservation staff) sadarkaa biyyaalessaa fi naannootti leenjii teeknikaa fi muuxannoo qabatamaa kennuu
  • Dargaggoota dursoomsuu: dargaggoota saayinsii lubbu-qabeenyaa keessatti barataniif sagantaa baruumsa olaanaa (fellowship) fi sagantaa muuxannoo hojii (internship) qabatamaa qopheessuun, hoggantoota eegumsa lubbu-qabeenyaa boruu uumuu
  • Hubannoo hawaasaa cimsuu: manneen barnootaa fi hawaasa naannoo keessatti sagantaa hubannoo eegumsa lubbu-qabeenyaa (wildlife conservation awareness programs) qopheessuun, ilaalcha hawaasaa lubbu-qabeenyaaf qaban fooyyessuu
  • Imaammata lubbu-qabeenyaa deeggaruu: imaammata adamoo (trophy hunting), daldala bineensotaa (wildlife trade) fi eegumsa iddoo jireenyaa (habitat protection) irratti, ragaa qorannoo qabatamaa fi falmii (advocacy) ragaa irratti hundaa'e dhiyeessuu
  • Qorannoo gaggeessuu fi maxxansuu: naannoolee adda addaa keessatti qorannoo lubbu-qabeenyaa fi bineensotaa gaggeessuun, bu'aa isaa journaalota saayinsii idil-addunyaa irratti maxxansiisuu fi beekumsa biyyaalessaa cimsuu
  • Waltajjii idil-addunyaa keessatti hirmaachuu: waltajjiiwwan idil-addunyaa, kanneen akka Convention on Biological Diversity (CBD) fi Convention on International Trade in Endangered Species (CITES), keessatti Itoophiyaa bakka bu'uun, fedhii biyyaalessaa kabachiisuu fi muuxannoo idil-addunyaa biyyatti fiduu

🔗 4. Sagantaalee fi Seektaroota Birootti Walitti Hidhamiinsa

🌱 Green Legacy (Ashaaraa Magariisaa) waliin walitti hidhamiinsa

Sagantaan Ashaaraa Magariisaa (Green Legacy Initiative), kan biqiltuu biiliyoona 48 ol dhaabuun seenaa addunyaa galmeessise, eegumsa lubbu-qabeenya bal'aa Itoophiyaaf carraa addaa kan banu yoo ta'u, bosonni haaromfamu fi lafti deebisanii dhaabame, bineensota bosonaa kanneen iddoo jireenya isaanii dhabaniif naannoo jireenyaa (habitat) haaraa fi mijataa uuma; akkasumas, wal-keessummeessaa lubbu-qabeenyaa cimaa fooyyessuun, lubbu-qabeenyaan badhaadhuu Itoophiyaa baroota dheeraaf akka itti fufu mirkaneessa. AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara kana keessatti biqiltuun dhaabamu hundi qooda eegumsa lubbu-qabeenyaa qabu akka ta'uuf, gosa biqiltuu naannoof mijatu fi naannummaa qabu (indigenous/native species) dursoomsuun saayinsiidhaan deeggaruu, biqiltuu karaa bineensonni walitti dhufanii sosoocho'an (wildlife corridors) keessatti dhaabuu, akkasumas iddoowwan haaromfaman keessatti bineensonni deebi'anii akka jiraatan hordoffii saayinsaawaa gaggeessuu irratti xiyyeeffachuun hojjeta. Karaa kanaan, sagantaan Green Legacy bosona haaromsuu qofa osoo hin taane, bineensotaa fi lubbu-qabeenya bal'aaf "mana haaraa" (new home) kan uumu ta'uun, eegumsa naannoo, deebii jijjiirama qilleensaa fi misooma hawaasummaa walumaan dhugoomsa.

🌳 REDD+ fi Saayinsii Bosonaa waliin walitti hidhamiinsa

Bosona tiksuun bineensota tiksuu wajjin walitti hidhamiinsa cimaa fi kallattii kan qabu yoo ta'u, lamaan keessaa tokko malee kan biraa milkaa'ina argachuu hin danda'u; sababiinsaas, bosonni iddoo jireenyaa (habitat) bineensota bosonaaf yoo ta'u, bineensonnis sirna ekoosistemaa bosonaa madaalaa fi fayya-qabeessa eeguuf gahee murteessaa qabu. AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara kana keessatti sirni REDD+ kuusaa kaarboonii dabaluu fi manca'iinsa bosonaa hir'isuu qofa osoo hin taane, eegumsa lubbu-qabeenya bal'aas akka deeggaru taasisuuf, sirna eegumsaa lubbu-qabeenyaa (biodiversity safeguards) sirna REDD+ keessatti hojiirra oolchuu irratti hojjeta. Karaa kanaan, hordoffii baay'ina bineensotaa, gabaasaa madaalawaa fi madaallii qulqullina iddoo jireenya bineensotaa (habitat quality monitoring) gaggeessuun, hojiin REDD+ lubbu-qabeenyaaf miidhaa malee bu'aa qabatamaa akka argamsiisu mirkaneessa. Akkasumas, gama biraatiin, bineensonni bosonaa fi tuuriizimiin uumamaa galii hawaasaaf maddisiisuu danda'an taasisuun, hawaasni naannoo bosona tiksuuf kaka'umsa diinagdee qabatamaa akka qabaatu mijeessuun, eegumsa bosonaa, kaarboonii fi lubbu-qabeenyaa walumaan dhugoomsa.

🌍 NRM fi Dandamannaa Jijjiirama Qilleensaa waliin walitti hidhamiinsa

Bineensotaa fi ekoosistemaa tiksuun, kallattiidhaan dandeettii dandamachuu jijjiirama qilleensaa biyyaalessaa cimsuun gahee guddaa qaba. Sababiinsaas, ekoosistemni fayya-qabeessi qulqullina bishaanii eegsisuu, dhukkubuu biyyee ittisuu, kuusaa kaarboonii ta'uu fi madaala qilleensa naannoo eegsisuu keessatti bu'uura. Tooftaan dandamannaa ekoosistemaa irratti hundaa'e (Ecosystem-based Adaptation), kan bosona, sululaa fi iddoo jireenya bineensotaa tiksuun karaa qilleensa jijjiiramaa biraa nagaadhaan dabarsu. AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara kana fi Sagantaa Dandamannaa Jijjiirama Qilleensaa gidduutti walitti hidhamiinsa cimaa fi waliigaltee ifa ta'e uuma. AFOLU Itoophiyaan keessumattuu lubbu-qabeenyi naannoo keessatti baay'inaan akka jiraatuu fi gosti murteessoo (keystone species), kanneen ekoosistema keessatti gahee gurguddaa kan akka biqiltuu facaasuu, dhalaa dhalaaf bishaan kuusuu fi bineensota biroo to'achuu qaban, sirritti akka tikfaman taasisuun, jiraachisaa fi madaalli ekoosistemaa qabatamaadhaan cimsa. Karaa kanaan, eegumsi lubbu-qabeenyaa qaama tarsiimoo dandamannaa jijjiirama qilleensaa biyyaalessaa kan ta'u yoo ta'u, hawaasni baadiyyaa fi qotee bultoonni jijjiirama qilleensaaf saaxilamoo ta'an, deeggarsa ekoosistemaa qabatamaa argachuun jireenya isaanii fooyyeffachuu danda'u.

"AFOLU Itoophiyaan seektara Bineensota Bosonaa fi Tuuriizimii keessatti pilaatfoormii beekumsaa fi qindoominaa ta'uun, hawaasa naannoo, qorattoota saayinsii fi qaamolee mootummaa walitti hidhuun, lubbu-qabeenya Itoophiyaa kan badiif saaxilamee jiru tiksa. Hawaasni paarkii fi naannoo eegumsa cinaa jiraatu galii qabatamaa tuuriizimii uumamaa irraa argachuun, eegumsi naannoo fi misoomni jireenya hawaasaa wal-cinaan akka guddatan haala mijeessa. lafti yoo tikfamte, namni nagaan jiraata, namni yoo nagaan jiraate, lafa tiksa'. Kanaaf, lubbu-qabeenya tiksuu fi jireenya hawaasaa fooyyessuun foncaa wal-cinaan deemu, kan tokkoon isaanii kan biraa malee hin milkoofnedha."

"Yeeyyiin Itoophiyaa dachee abbaa isaa Baalee keessatti bilisaan kaachuu, jaldeessi geelada Simien keessatti yaadda'a malee jiraachuu, kun kennaa osoo hin taane, mirga uumamaan kennameef ti. Mirga kana tiksuun aangoo osoo hin taane, dirqama dhaloota har'aa ti. Bineensota keenyaan boonuu, kun jalqabuma; tiksuu fi haala isaaniif mijatu uumuu, kun dhugoomsuu dha. Gaaffiin guddaan, 'Boruu, ijoolleen keenya seenaa kana kitaaba keessatti dubbisumoo, ykn ijaan arguu?' kan jedhu dha."

"The Ethiopian wolf to roam free on its native soil , and the gelada to graze unburdened in the Simien, these are not gifts, but rights bestowed by nature itself. To safeguard these rights is not authority, but the moral duty of this generation. Pride in our wildlife is merely the beginning; protection and the creation of conditions where they may thrive, that is the fulfillment. The greater question remains: 'Will our children, tomorrow, read this story in books, or witness it with their own eyes?'"

🌱 1. Sagantichi Maali — What is Green Legacy?

🇪🇹 Afaan Oromoo

Sagantaa Ashaaraa Magariisaa Itoophiyaa

Sagantaan Ashaaraa Magariisaa inisheetivii haaromsa naannoo biyyaalessaa bara 2019 hundeeffame dha. Kaayyoon isaa guddaan haguuggii bosona biyyattii 30% tti ga'uu, lafa manca'e hektaara miliyoona 20+ haaromsuu fi lammilee miliyoonaan sagantaadhaan hirmaachisuu dha. Inisheetiviin kun seenaa galmeessera — guyyaa tokkotti biqiltuu miliyoona 350+ dhaabame, addunyaatti record ta'e.

Sagantichi biqiltuu dhaabuu qofa miti — lafa manca'e haaromsuu, bishaan tiksuuu, biodiversitii dagaachiisuu fi jireenya hawaasaa fooyyessuu walitti makuun hojjeta. Biqiltuuwwan firiilee (5–10%) fi bosona (90–95%) walitti makuun, sagantaan wabii nyaataa fi madda galii dabalataa hawaasaaf argamsiisuu irrattis xiyyeeffata.

🌍 English

The Sagantaa Dhaalota Magariisa (Green Legacy Initiative) is Ethiopia's most ambitious and high-profile environmental restoration program. Launched in 2019, the initiative set out to plant billions of seedlings across Ethiopia to restore degraded landscapes, reverse deforestation, and contribute to the global fight against climate change. In its first year alone, Ethiopia planted over 350 million trees in a single day — setting a world record.

Since then, the initiative has continued expanding, reaching over 48 billion seedlings planted across all of Ethiopia's regions. The program is uniquely community-driven, mobilizing millions of Ethiopians — from schoolchildren and farmers to government officials — in large-scale planting events that combine ecological restoration with national civic engagement and rural livelihood improvement.

🔬 2. AFOLU fi Green Legacy — Deeggarsa Saayinsaawaa

AFOLU Itoophiyaa Green Legacy Akkamitti Deeggaraa?

AFOLU Itoophiyaa sagantaa Green Legacy keessatti pilaatfoormii beekumsaa ta'uun gahee ol-aanaa qaba. Sagantichi dhaabuu qofaa osoo hin taane, biqiltuun dhaabamte jiraachuu fi bu'aa argamsiisuu mirkaneessuuf saayinsii, qorannoo fi muuxannoo gadi-fageenyaan barbaachisa. AFOLU gaheelee armaan gadii guuta:

Species selection saayinsaawaa — biqiltuun naannoo tokkoon tokkotti madaqte akka dhaabamtu mirkaneessuu; nursery quality — biqiltuu qulqulluu fi cimtu qopheessuu; survival rate hordofuu — dhaabame meeqni jiraate madaaluuu; fi bu'aa ecological — carbon, biodiversitii fi bishaanii — maddisiisuu irratti hojjeta.

🔬 3. Hojiwwan Ijoo 6 — AFOLU's Key Roles in Green Legacy

01
🧬
Species Filatuu fi Nursery Saayinsiin Deeggaruu
Science-Based Species Selection & Nursery Quality Support

Biqiltuun dhaabamtu naannoo tokkoon tokkotti madaquu qabdi — goggogaa keessatti drought-tolerant, ol-aanaa keessatti naannoo sanitti beekamutu dhaabama. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti ragaa saayinsaawaa fayyadamuun species selection fi nursery quality mirkaneessuu irratti hojjeta.

  • Naannoolee agroecological tokkoon tokkoo species malli madaqaa dha adda baasuu
  • Native fi indigenous species dursa kennuu — biodiversitii tiksuuf
  • Nursery management standards — quality seedlings mirkaneessuu — qopheessuu
  • Drought-tolerant fi climate-resilient species goggogaa keessatti babal'isuu
  • Firiilee (5–10%) fi bosona species sirriitti balance gochuuf qajeelcha
  • Species diversity — monoculture hin ta'iin, gosa garaagaraa makuu — cimsu
02
📊
Survival Rate Hordofuu fi Madaallii
Survival Rate Monitoring, Verification & Assessment

Biqiltuu dhaabame miliyoonaan lakkaa'amu keessaa meeqni jiraate? Kuni beekuu baay'ee barbaachisa — sagantaan bu'aa fidaa jiraa jechuuf. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti MRV systems diriirfachuun, survival rate fi growth monitoring irratti hojjeta.

  • Survival rate assessment sirna tokkoffaa fi lammaffaa (1yr, 2yr) dhaabuu
  • Field surveys fi drone/satellite imagery walitti makuun hordofuu
  • Mobile data collection apps fayyadamuun rapid assessment gaggeessuu
  • Growth measurement — height, DBH, canopy cover — yeroo yeroon hordofuu
  • Naannoolee survival rate gadi-aanaa — rakkoo adda baasuu fi furmaata
  • Gabaasaalee mootummaaf fi idil-addunyaadhaaf evidence-based dhiyeessuu
03
💨
Carbon Kuusuu Maddisiisuu fi REDD+ Deeggaruu
Carbon Stock Assessment & REDD+ Integration

Biqiltuun dhaabamte carbon meeqa kuusaa? Kuni madaaluun biyyattiin waadaa galtee — NDC keessatti — guutaa jirtii mirkaneessuu fi galii carbon irraa argachuuf barbaachisa. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti carbon accounting fi REDD+ walitti hidhuu irratti hojjeta.

  • Above fi below-ground biomass carbon stock assessment sirna diriirfachuu
  • Allometric equations Ethiopia-specific qopheessuu fi hojiirra oolchuu
  • NDC kaayyoo keessatti Green Legacy bu'aa galmeessuu deeggaruu
  • Voluntary carbon markets fi compliance markets walitti hidhuu
  • Hawaasni carbon credits irraa galii argachuu sirna dhaabuu
  • UNFCCC fi Paris Agreement irratti Itoophiyaa gabaasa deeggaruu
04
🌊
Bu'aa Ecological Madaallii — Ecosystem Benefits
Ecological Impact Assessment — Water, Soil & Biodiversity

Green Legacy sagantaa bu'aa ecological meeqa fida? Bishaanii dabalaa jiraa? Biyyeen fooyyachaa jiraa? Biodiversitii deebi'aa jiraa? AFOLU seektara kana keessatti bu'aa ecological sagantichaa maddisiisuu fi gabaasuu irratti hojjeta.

  • Watershed hydrology jijjiirama — haromoo fi laga haaromuu — hordofuu
  • Soil erosion fi fertility jijjiirama biqiltuu dhaabame naannoo keessatti
  • Biodiversity recovery — bineensota fi simbiroo deebi'uu — hordofuu
  • Micro-climate jijjiirama — temperature fi humidity — measurement
  • Long-term ecological monitoring plots Green Legacy naannoo keessatti
  • Ecosystem services valuation — carbon, water, biodiversity — maddisiisuu
05
🍎
Firiilee fi Wabii Nyaataa Walitti Hidhuuu
Fruit Trees Integration & Food Security Contribution

Biqiltuuwwan dhaabaman keessaa 5–10% firiilee ta'uu kaayyeffama — kuni wabii nyaataa fi galii qonnaan bulaa irratti dhiibbaa guddaa qaba. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti firiilee species filatuu, nursery quality fi hawaasaaf raabsuu mirkaneessuu irratti hojjeta.

  • Firiilee species — Avocado, Papaya, Mango, Apple, Citrus — filatuu fi raabsuu
  • Hawaasni firiilee species barbaadu adda baasuu fi qopheessuu
  • Firiilee dhaabame kunuunsa jalqabaa — watering, weeding — leenjii kennuu
  • Wabii nyaataa irratti Green Legacy bu'aa — diverse food sources — maddisiisuu
  • Firiilee galii — selling, processing — value chain walitti hidhuu
  • Nutrition diversity — vitamins, minerals — firiilee irraa argachuu
06
🤝
Hawaasa Hirmaachisuu fi Ijaarsa Dandeettii
Community Mobilization, Capacity Building & Ownership

Green Legacy hawaasni of-danda'ee hogganu fi tiksu ta'uu barbaachisa — sagantaan xumuramuu boodas dhaabama jiraachuu. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti hawaasa gurmeessuu, leenjisuu fi sagantichaan itti gaafatamummaa kennuu irratti hojjeta.

  • Garee hawaasaa (Community Planting Groups) ijaaruu fi leenjisuu
  • Dubartii fi dargaggoo sagantaa keessatti dursa kennuu fi hirmaachisuu
  • Schools fi dhaabbilee barnootaa Green Legacy leenjii fi hirmaannaa
  • Local champions — muuxannoo qaban — adda baasuu fi naannoo isaaniif fayyadamuu
  • Annual planting events qopheessuu fi mobilization cimsu
  • Muuxannoo milkaa'inaa naannoolee gidduutti daddabarsuu fi waltajjii

📅 4. Seenaa Milkaa'inaa — Green Legacy Timeline

2019
350M
🏆 Jalqabaa fi World Record — Inisheetiviin eegale
Addunyaatti record — guyyaa tokkotti biqiltuu miliyoona 350 dhaabame. Haguuggii bosona biyyattii 15% ture. Itoophiyaan haaluma kanaan, naannoolee 11 keessatti hirmaannaan guddaa ture.
2020
5B+
🌳 Dagaaguu itti fufe — COVID dhiibbaa jala
COVID-19 hordofaa, sagantaan itti fufe. Biqiltuu biiliyoona 5+ waggaa kana dhaabame. Hawaasni naannoo hundaa hirmaate. AFOLU survival rate monitoring eegale.
2021
7.5B
🌿 Kaayyoo guddaa — Haguuggii 20% ga'e
Haguuggii bosona 20% darbee. Waggaa kana biqiltuu biiliyoona 7.5 dhaabame. Firiilee species babal'isuu fi wabii nyaataa walitti hidhuu sirni eegale.
2022
20B+
📈 Gara biiliyoonaan — biqiltuun cumaha darbite
Biqiltuu biiliyoona 20+ dhaabamte — waggaalee hunda caalaa. Lammilee 767,000+ carraa hojii argatan. Carbon sequestration assessment jalqabame. Haguuggii 21.5% ga'e.
2023
32B+
🌍 Addunyaa irratti beekame — NDC deeggarsa
Biqiltuu biiliyoona 32+ ga'e. Paris Agreement NDC keessatti Green Legacy bu'aa galmeeffame. International recognition baay'ate. AFOLU carbon methodology qopheessuu eegale.
2024
40B+
🏆 Haguuggii 23.6% — Kaayyoo 30% irratti hojiin jira
Biqiltuu biiliyoona 40+ dhaabame. Haguuggii bosona 23.6% ga'e. Ecosystem recovery — watershed, biodiversity — maddisiifame. Kaayyoo 2030 — 30% — irratti tarkaanfiin guddaan fudhatame.
2025+
48B+
🎯 Itti fufa — Kaayyoo 30% 2030
Biqiltuu biiliyoona 48+ ga'eera. Itti fufa — waggaatti biiliyoonaan dhaabuu. Haguuggii 30% 2030 ga'uu kaayyoo biyyaalessaa. AFOLU saayinsii fi monitoring cimsuun sagantaa deeggaraa jira.

🌳 5. Species Biqiltuu Ijoo — Key Tree Species Planted

Species diversity Green Legacy bu'uura. AFOLU seektarichi species selection saayinsiin utubee, naannoo tokkoon tokkotti madaqe hojjeta.

🌲
Eucalyptus (Baarfuu)
Eucalyptus globulus & spp.
Saffisaan guddatu, qoraa fi lafa tiksuuf gargaara. Naannoolee qonnaan bulaan beekamu dha. Garuu monoculture hanqina qabaachuu danda'a — AFOLU native species waliin balance gochuuf gorsa.
📊 ~40% biqiltuu dhaabame keessaa
🌳
Acacia (Waacu)
Acacia spp. (various)
Naannoolee goggogaa fi dirree keessatti baay'ee beekama. Nitrogen-fixing ta'uun biyyee fooyyessa. Fodder, gumii fi bosona tiksuuf bu'aa guddaa qaba.
🌿 Goggogaa naannoo — Afaar, Somaalee
🥑
Avokaadoo (Avocado)
Persea americana
Firiilee ijoo — wabii nyaataa fi galii. Inisheetivii Bulee waliin qindaawee miliyoona 10+ qonnaan bulaadhaaf raabsame. Naannoolee giddu-galeessaa fi ol-aanaa keessatti baay'ee madaqeera.
🍎 Firiilee — miliyoona 10+ raabsame
🍌
Paappayyaa (Papaya)
Carica papaya
Saffisaan firiilee kenna — waggaa 1 keessatti. Wabii nyaataa fi galii yeroo gabaabaatti argamsiisa. Naannoolee giddu-galeessaa keessatti milkaa'a. Hawaasni dhiyoo fayyadama.
🍌 Firiilee — waggaa 1 keessatti
🌿
Sesbania (N-Fixing)
Sesbania sesban
Nitrogen-fixing ta'uun biyyee fooyyessa — qonnaan walitti makuun. Saffisaan guddatu, fodder fi fuel wood kennaa. Agroforestry keessatti baay'ee bu'aa qabeessa ta'e.
🌱 NRM + Agroforestry — species ijoo
☕
Shade Trees + Buna
Coffee shade species
Bosona buna keessa species — Grevillea, Albizia — buna gahaannisa jala oomishuuf. SNNPR fi Oromiyaa keessatti Green Legacy fi buna oomisha walitti makuun hojjetama.
☕ SNNPR fi Oromiyaa — shade coffee

✨ 6. Bu'aawwan Guguddoo — Multidimensional Benefits

💨
Kaarboonii Kuusuu — Carbon Sequestration
Biqiltuun dhaabamte CO₂ kuusuun jijjiirama qilleensaa hir'isuu irratti gahee ol-aanaa qaba. NDC kaayyoo Itoophiyaa guutuu fi climate finance argachuuf bu'uura.
💧
Bishaan Tiksuuu — Water Regulation
Bosoni rooba qabsiisuun, haromoo guutuun fi bishaan lafa jalaa guddisuu keessatti gahee olaanaa qaba. Laga fi haromoo haaromsuu sagantaa kanarraa milkaa'uu eegame.
🌍
Biyyee Tiksuuu — Soil Conservation
Muka dhaabamtu biyyee roobaan butamuu ittisuu, biyyee manmantii fooyyessuun, fi lafa manca'e haaromsuu irratti gahee guddaa qaba. Oomishtummaa lafaa yeroo dheeraa mirkaneessa.
🦋
Biodiversitii — Biodiversity Recovery
Bosoni haaromfame bineensota, simbiroo fi lubbu-qabeeyyii biroo irroof naannoo jireenyaa haaraa uuma. Genetic diversity fi ecosystem resilience cimsa.
💰
Galii fi Jireenya — Livelihoods
Lammilee 767,000+ carraa hojii argate. Firiilee fi NTFPs madda galii dabalataa. Nursery fi planting work hawaasa baadiyyaa fayyadama.
🌡
Dandamannaa Qilleensaa — Resilience
Bosona fi landscape haaromfame jijjiirama qilleensaatti dandamuuf hawaasaa fi naannoo dandeettii guddisa. Micro-climate fooyyessuun qonnaa deeggaraa.

Bosona qiltu		 Native forest species, Shade trees, Papaya Bosona hedduu hafe — tiksuun bu'uura Forest conservation + buna quality CFM Biodiversity
🏔 Tigray
Haaromsa naannoo		 Acacia, Doddona, Olea, Drought-tolerant species Lafa baay'ee manca'aa — restoration ta'aa jira Dryland restoration, SWC waliin Restoration science
🏜 Afaar fi Somaalee
Goggogaa		 Acacia senegal, Balanites, Commiphora Dryland species — drought tolerance ijoo Dryland GL — water harvesting waliin Drought tolerance Survival focus

🔗 8. Seektaroota fi Sagantaalee Walitti Hidhiinsa

🌳 Saayinsii Bosonaa waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Green Legacy milkaa'uuf Saayinsii Bosonaa bu'uura. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti species selection saayinsaawaa, forest inventory, carbon stock assessment, fi survival monitoring hundi Saayinsii Bosonaa irraa maddu. Bosonnii haaromfame akkamitti jiraatu fi guddatu — kuni Saayinsii Bosonaa irratti hundaa'a.

🌍 NRM fi Agroforestirii waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Green Legacy biqiltuu dhaabuu qofa osoo hin taane — biyyee tiksuuu, sulula haaromsuu fi ekoosistema deebisuu. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti SWC structures irratti biqiltuu dhaabuu, agroforestry systems keessatti makuu, fi watershed restoration waliin qindaa'uu mirkaneessuu irratti hojjeta.

🌾 Wabii Nyaataa fi Saayinsii Biqiltootaa waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Firiilee (5–10%) Green Legacy keessatti dhaabamtu wabii nyaataa fi galii qonnaan bulaa irratti dhiibbaa guddaa qaba. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti firiilee species quality fi raabsuu, nutrition diversity mirkaneessuu, fi Inisheetivii Bulee waliin qindaa'uu irratti hojjeta.

🌾 1. Sagantichi Maali — What is Food Security at AFOLU?

🇪🇹 Afaan Oromoo

Sagantaa Wabii Nyaataa fi Sirna Nyaataa AFOLU Itoophiyaa

Wabii nyaataa jechuun nyaatni yeroo hunda, naannoo hunda, fi hawaasni hundi — baay'ina, qulqullina fi gosa — gahaa argachuu danda'u jechuu dha. Itoophiyaa keessatti rakkoon wabii nyaataa hedduu baay'ee — rooba gahaa dhabuu, biyyee manca'uu, gabaa dhaqqabuu dadhabuu, hir'ina teknolojii, fi jijjiirama qilleensaa — walitti hidhamani dhufan.

AFOLU Itoophiyaa sagantaa kana keessatti seektaroota teknikaa hunda — Saayinsii Biqiltootaa, Beelladootaa, Agroforestirii fi Misoomaa Baadiyyaa — walitti maknaan furmaata walga'aa dhiyeessa. Sagantaan inisheetiviiwwan biyyaalessaa guguddoo — Qamadii, Faaya, Bulee — deeggaruun milkaa'ina oomishtummaa guddinaa keessatti ragaa teknikaa fi beekumsa dhiyeessuuf hojjeta.

🌍 English

Food security remains one of Ethiopia's most pressing development challenges. Despite significant agricultural potential, millions of Ethiopians face seasonal food insecurity driven by drought, land degradation, poor market access, and climate variability. AFOLU Ethiopia's food security program addresses these challenges through integrated, multi-sector interventions that simultaneously improve agricultural production, natural resource management, and market linkages.

By integrating AFOLU's technical sectors — including plant science, animal science, agroforestry, and rural development — the food security program builds resilient food systems that can withstand both environmental and economic shocks. The program particularly focuses on the most vulnerable communities, including female-headed households and smallholder farmers in climate-stressed regions.

🚀 2. Inisheetiviiwwan Biyyaalessaa Guguddoo — Key National Initiatives

AFOLU Itoophiyaa inisheetiviiwwan biyyaalessaa armaan gadii saayinsii fi beekumsaan deeggaruun, oomishtummaa guddisuu keessatti gahee olaanaa qaba.

🌾 Inisheetivii Qamadii
🌾
Inisheetivii Misooma Qamadii
Bara 2019 eegale. Qamadii bonaa jallisiin oomishuuf xiyyeeffachuun, Itoophiyaan oomisha qamadiitiin of danda'uun gabaa alaatiif erguu jalqabde. Kuni seenaa keessatti milkaa'ina guddaa dha.
  • Lafa hektaara miiliyoona 3+ qamadii bonaa jallisiin misoomfame
  • Oomishni kuntaala M 50 irraa M 110 olitti guddate
  • Itoophiyaan qamadii import dhaabuun 2023 irraa export eegalte
  • Sanyii ammayyaa drought-tolerant fi high-yield babal'ifame
  • Sharafa alaa argamsiisuu keessatti gahee guddaa qaba
3M+
Heektaara irrigated wheat
🥛 Yelemat Tirufat (Faaya)
🐄
Inisheetivii Faaya — Yelemat Tirufat
Bara 2022 eegale. Misooma beelladaa ammayyeessuun oomishtummaa foonii, aannanii, hanqaaquu fi dammaa guddisuu irratti argannoo guddaa galmeesseera. Sirna nyaataa madaalawaa hawaasaa fooyyessuu.
  • Aannaan L biiliyoona 11.7 → 14.1 guddate
  • Hanqaaquu biiliyoona 1.5 → 2.2 guddate
  • Dammaa toonii 112K → 147K guddate
  • Foon toonii 400K+ gabaa gahee jira
  • Jireenya hawaasaa baadiyyaa jijjiiruun wabii nyaataa mirkaneessaa
14.1B
Litira aannanii/waggaa
🥑 Inisheetivii Bulee
🥑
Inisheetivii Bulee — Green Fruit & Vegetable
Bara 2019/2020 eegale. Kuduraa, muduraa fi biqiltoota mi'eessituu ammayyeessuun oomishtummaa gabaa irratti xiyyeeffate guddisuu. Madda galii fi wabii nyaataa madaalawaa mirkaneessuuf.
  • Kuduraa fi muduraa hektaara 800K+ irratti bal'ate
  • Waggaatti kuntaala M 70+ gabaa biyyaa fi alaatiif
  • Avokaadoo fi Paappayyaa miliyoona 10+ raabsame
  • Sharafa alaa argamsiisuu fi dorgommii guddisuu
  • Dubartii fi maatii hiyyeeyyii fayyadama keessatti xiyyeeffame
800K+
Heektaara horticulture
🤝 Deeggarsa Hawaasaa
🛡
Neetwoorkii Deeggarsa Hawaasaa — Safety Nets & Social Protection
Hawaasota balaa nyaataa jala jiran — dubartii hoggantuu maatii, hiyyeeyyii fi godinaalee qilleensa miidhamaniif — deeggarsa hatattamaa fi dheeraa kennuu. AFOLU kana tti gorsa fi ragaa teknikaa dhiyeessa.
  • PSNP (Productive Safety Net Programme) deeggarsa teknikaa
  • Emergency food assistance naannoolee balaa keessatti
  • Nutrition-sensitive agriculture programs hawaasaaf
  • Cash transfer fi in-kind support programs
  • Resilience building — jireenya dheeraa mirkaneessuu
8M+
Namoota PSNP deeggaree

🔬 3. Hojiwwan Ijoo 6 — Key Program Activities

01
🧬
Teknolojii Qonnaa fi Sanyii Ammayyaa Babal'isuu
Improved Agricultural Technology & Seed Access for Smallholders

Sanyii ammayyaa fi teknolojii qonnaa babal'isuu — qonnaan bulaan oomishtummaa akka guddisan mirkaneessuu. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti ragaa saayinsaawaa dhiyeessuun inisheetiviiwwan biyyaalessaa deeggaruu irratti hojjeta.

  • Sanyii qamadii, boqqolloo, teff fi midhaan callaa biroo ammayyaa babal'isuu
  • Jallisii teknolojii — micro-irrigation, sprinkler, drip — qonnaan bulaan argatuu
  • Fertilizer fi agrochemicals sirriitti fayyadamuu leenjii kennuu
  • Climate-smart agriculture (CSA) practices — drought-tolerant varieties
  • Mechanization — tractor, harvester — collective use schemes dhaabuu
  • Post-harvest teknolojii — storage, drying — loss hir'isuuf babal'isuu
02
🌍
Haaromsa Qabeenya Uumamaa fi Lafa Manca'e Deebisuu
Natural Resource Rehabilitation for Agricultural Recovery

Lafa manca'e haaromsuu — biyyee fi bishaanii tiksuun qonnaa gara oomishtummaa ol-aanaa fi itti fufiinsaatti ceesisuu. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti NRM fi Agroforestirii waliin ta'uun lafa haaromsuu fi oomisha guddisuu irratti hojjeta.

  • Watershed rehabilitation — sulula qonnaa manca'e haaromsuu
  • Soil fertility restoration — manmantii fi conservation tillage
  • Agroforestry integration — muka nitrogen-fixing qonnaa keessatti
  • Irrigation infrastructure — mana bishaanii fi canals — dhaabuu
  • Rangeland rehabilitation — horsiisee fi qonnaan bulaa lachuu fayyadama
  • Land use planning — lafa qonnaan babal'isuu fi bosona tiksuuu balance
03
🏪
Gabaa Walitti Hidhuu fi Post-Harvest Loss Hir'isuu
Market Linkage & Post-Harvest Loss Reduction

Oomishni guddachuu qofaa gahaa miti — gabaa gahuu fi bu'aa haqa qabu argachuu barbaachisa. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti qonnaan bulaa gabaa walitti hidhuu, post-harvest loss hir'isuu fi value addition cimsu irratti hojjeta.

  • Storage technologies — metallic silos, hermetic bags — babal'isuu
  • Collective marketing — kooperatiivii fi garee — deeggaruu fi cimsu
  • Processing fi value addition — milling, packaging — cimsu
  • Market information systems — gatii fi gabaa odeeffannoo — raabsuu
  • Cold chain fi logistics rakkoo adda baasuu fi furmaata kennuu
  • Food safety standards — quality control — qonnaan bulaan barsiisuu
04
🥗
Qonnaa Nyaata Madaalawaa fi Diversification
Nutrition-Sensitive Agriculture & Dietary Diversification

Nyaatni madaalawaa — carbohydrates qofa osoo hin taane, proteins, vitamins fi minerals dabalatee — barbaachisaa dha. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti diversified food systems — midhaan callaa, beelladaa, firiilee fi kuduraa — irratti hojjeta.

  • Homestead food production — kuduraa fi firiilee mana keessatti oomisuu
  • Small livestock — lukkuu, re'ee, dammaa — hawaasaaf babal'isuu
  • Biofortification — iron, zinc, vitamin A rich varieties — babal'isuu
  • Nutrition education fi behavior change communication
  • School feeding programs — hawaasaa fi government waliin hojjechuu
  • Infant fi child feeding practices fooyyeessuuf leenjii fi awareness
05
🛡
Deeggarsa Hawaasaa fi Social Protection
Safety Net & Social Protection Integration

Hawaasota gar malee miidhamani — dubartii hoggantuu maatii, hiyyeeyyii, naannoolee balaa keessa jiran — wabii nyaataa mirkaneessuuf deeggarsa hatattamaa fi dheeraa barbaachisa. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti gorsa teknikaa fi ragaa dhiyeessa.

  • PSNP (Productive Safety Net Programme) irratti deeggarsa teknikaa
  • Emergency food response — famine early warning — deeggaruu
  • Resilience building — jireenya dheeraa fi diversification
  • Dubartii fi hawaasota miidhamaniif sagantaa dursa kennuu
  • Cash fi food transfers — balaa yeroo — sirna qopheessuu
  • Livelihood diversification — madda galii hedduu uumuu
06
📊
Hordofuu Wabii Nyaataa fi Ragaa Dhiyeessuu
Food Security Monitoring, Data & Policy Support

Wabii nyaataa haala meeqa dha? Naannoo kamiitu rakkoo cimaa qaba? Inisheetiviiwwan bu'aa fidaa jiruu? — gaaffiiwwan kanneen deebii argachuuf hordofuu fi madaallii barbaachisa. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti ragaa saayinsaawaa mootummaaf dhiyeessuu hojjeta.

  • Food security surveys fi assessments naannoolee keessatti gaggeessuu
  • FEWS NET fi Early Warning Systems deeggaruu fi ragaa dhiyeessuu
  • Nutrition surveys — stunting, wasting, underweight — hordofuu
  • Inisheetiviiwwan bu'aa — oomishtummaa guddinni — madaaluuu fi gabaasuu
  • Policy briefs fi recommendations mootummaaf qopheessuu
  • Addunyaa forums — WFP, FAO — keessatti Itoophiyaa bu'aa agarsiisuu

🥗 4. Nyaata Gosa Adda Addaa — Food Groups & Production Focus

🌾
Midhaan Callaa — Cereals
Wheat, Teff, Maize, Sorghum, Barley
Bu'uura nyaataa Itoophiyaa. Qamadii inisheetivii tiin kuntaala M 110 ga'eera. Teff injera irratti bu'uuraa. Boqqolloo fi sorghum goggogaa keessatti ijoo. AFOLU ragaa teknikaa fi sanyii ammayyaa dhiyeessa.
🌾 Qamadii: 50M → 110M kuntaala
🥛
Aannaan fi Biqiltuu Madda Protein — Dairy & Legumes
Milk, Eggs, Pulses, Beans, Lentils
Protein madda. Faaya inisheetivii tiin aannaan 14.1B litira ga'e. Hanqaaquu 2.2B+. Ataraa fi faasulyaa protein plant-based madda. AFOLU beelladaa fi legumes babal'isuu deeggaraa.
🥛 Aannaan: 11.7B → 14.1B litira
🥕
Kuduraa — Vegetables
Tomatoes, Onions, Carrots, Cabbage
Vitamins fi minerals madda. Bulee inisheetivii tiin hektaara 800K+ irratti bal'ate. Hawaasni maatii mana keessaa fi market garden irraa fayyadama. Nutrition diversity mirkaneessa.
🥕 Bulee: hektaara 800K+ oomishame
🥑
Firiilee — Fruits
Avocado, Banana, Mango, Papaya, Citrus
Vitamins, fiber fi galii dabalataa. Avokaadoo miliyoona 10+ raabsame. Green Legacy keessaa 5-10% firiilee species. Export potential ol-aanaa. AFOLU nursery fi value chain deeggaraa.
🥑 Avokaadoo: 10M+ raabsame
🥩
Foon fi Beeladaa Oomisha — Meat & Livestock
Beef, Mutton, Chicken, Honey
Iron, zinc fi protein guddaa madda. Faaya tiin foon toonii 400K+ gabaa gahee jira. Dammaa toonii 147K+. Horsiisee baadiyyaa keessatti jireenya ijoo.
🥩 Foon: toonii 400K+ · Dammaa: 147K
🌿
Biqiltoota Mi'eessituu — Spices & NTFPs
Coffee, Spices, Medicinal Plants
Buna, fenugreek, turmeric fi biqiltoota mi'eessituu biroo — galii fi nyaata madaalawaa irratti gahee qaba. Export potential guddaa. AFOLU value chain fi quality cimsu deeggaraa.
☕ Buna: $1.4B export galii/waggaa

🔄 5. Tartiiba Hojii — AFOLU's Integrated Approach

1
🔍
Haala Wabii Nyaataa Qorannoo — Food Security Assessment
Naannoo keessatti hawaasni hamma nyaataa barbaaduu argataa jiraa? Rakkoon eessaa madda? Dhabamni nyaataa seezonal dha moo waggaa guutuu? FEWS NET, household surveys fi nutrition data fayyadamuun haala sirriitti madaalama. Kuni karoora hunda bu'uura.
2
🌾
Oomishtummaa Guddisuu — Production Enhancement
Sanyii ammayyaa, jallisii, fertilizer fi teknolojii fayyadamuun oomishtummaa guddisuu. Inisheetiviiwwan biyyaalessaa — Qamadii, Faaya, Bulee — saayinsiin deeggaruun hojiin itti fufsiisuu.
3
🌱
Diversification fi Nutrition — Heddummina Nyaataa
Midhaan callaa qofa osoo hin taane — beelladaa, firiilee, kuduraa fi biqiltoota mi'eessituu walitti makuun, nyaatni madaalawaa fi heddumminaan argamu mirkaneessuu. Homestead garden fi small livestock hawaasaaf babal'isuu.
4
🏪
Gabaa fi Value Chain — Market Access
Oomishni guddachuu fi gabaa gahuu — lachuu mirkaneessuu barbaachisa. Post-harvest loss hir'isuu, storage fooyyeessuu, fi qonnaan bulaa gabaa kallattiin walitti hidhuu. Galii qonnaan bulaa guddisuun nyaata bitachuu dandeettii isaa ol guddisa.
5
🛡
Hawaasa Miidhamaniif Deeggarsa — Safety Nets
Hawaasota gar malee miidhamani — hiyyeeyyii, dubartii hoggantuu maatii, godinaalee balaa keessa jiran — hatattaman deeggaruu. PSNP fi emergency response waliin hojjechuun, eenyuun illee akka hin hafinee mirkaneessuu.
6
📊
Hordofuu fi Imaammataa — M&E & Policy
Bu'aan sagantichaa madaalamuun, imaammataa biyyaalessaa fooyyeessuuf ragaa saayinsaawaa dhiyeessuu. AFOLU evidence-based policy briefs mootummaaf kennu — sagantaalee haaraa karoorsuu fi jiran fooyyeessuuf.

🗺 6. Naannoolee fi Haala Wabii Nyaataa — Regional Food Security Status

Naannoo / Region Rakkoo Ijoo Oomisha Ijoo Haala Nyaataa Xiyyeeffannoo AFOLU
🌾 Oromiyaa
Qonnaa guddaa		 Rooba gahaa dhabuu, biyyee manca'uu, gabaa Teff, Boqqolloo, Qamadii, Buna, Hortikulturaa Haala garaa garaa — naannoo tokko tokko rakkoo cimaa Wheat + Bulee Irrigation
🏔 Amaaraa
Oomisha teff		 Drought, lafa manca'uu, post-harvest loss Teff, Qamadii, Garbuu, Dinnicha Seezonal food gap — bonaa keessatti rakkoo Wheat Initiative NRM
🌿 SNNPR
Diversity guddaa		 Market access, post-harvest, gabaa geessuu Ensete, Buna, Firiilee, Spices, Hortikulturaa Ensete irratti hirkannaan baay'ee guddaa Diversification Coffee NTFPs
🏜 Afaar fi Somaalee
Pastoral		 Drought cimaa, bishaan dhabuu, market dhaqqabuu Loon, Gaangee, Foon fi Aannaan Rakkoo cimaa — acute food insecurity baay'ee Emergency food Resilience
🏔 Tigray
Haaromsa		 Confict recovery, lafa manca'uu, infrastructure Qamadii, Sorghum, Teff, Loon Recovery phase — restoration fi rebuilding Recovery support Restoration

🔗 7. Seektaroota fi Sagantaalee Walitti Hidhiinsa

🌾 Saayinsii Biqiltootaa waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Wabii nyaataa mirkaneessuuf oomishtummaa guddisuu — Saayinsii Biqiltootaa irratti hundaa'a. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti sanyii ammayyaa drought-tolerant babal'isuu, jallisii fi agroonoomii teknolojii, fi post-harvest loss hir'isuu irratti qorannoo fi gorsa kennuu irratti hojjeta. Inisheetivii Qamadii bu'uuruma kana irratti hundaa'e.

🐄 Saayinsii Beelladootaa fi Faaya waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Nyaatni madaalawaa — protein, aannaan, foon fi hanqaaquu — mirkaneessuuf Saayinsii Beelladootaa fi Inisheetivii Faaya ijoo dha. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti sanyii fooyyeffame, nyaata beelladootaa cimsu fi fayyaa beelladootaa mirkaneessuu — aannaan 14.1B, hanqaaquu 2.2B fi foon 400K+ oomishamuuf ragaa teknikaa dhiyeessuuf hojjeta.

🌡 Dandamannaa Jijjiirama Qilleensaa waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Jijjiiramni qilleensaa wabii nyaataa irratti balaa guddaa qabu — droughtii dabaluu, roobni gahaa dhabuu, fi extreme weather events oomisha ni miidhanu. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti Climate-Smart Agriculture (CSA) practices babal'isuu, drought-tolerant varieties dhiyeessuu fi early warning systems diriirfachuun dandamannaa food systems cimsu irratti hojjeta.

"AFOLU Itoophiyaa sagantaa Wabii Nyaataa fi Sirna Nyaataa keessatti seektaroota teknikaa hunda walitti makuun hojjeta — saayinsii biqiltootaa, beelladootaa, agroforestirii fi misoomaa baadiyyaa — rakkoota nyaataa Itoophiyaa keessatti mul'atan furmaata walga'aan deebisuuf. Nyaatni gahaan, madaalawaan fi hunda dhaqqabaan — kuni mirga hawaasni Itoophiyaa hundi qabu."

"Namni beekumsa, sanyii fi deeggarsa argannaan — lafa tokkicha irraa maatii isaatii fi biyya isaa nyaachisu. Wabii nyaataa jechuun nyaatni gahaan, madaalawaan fi guyyaa guyyaan dhaqqabamu mirga dhalootaa ta'uu qaba."

"When a farmer receives knowledge, seed, and support — they can feed their family and their country from the same small plot of land. Food security means that adequate, nutritious, and daily access to food must be a birthright, not a privilege."

AFOLU Itoophiyaa — Wabii Nyaataa fi Sirna Nyaataa · Food Security Program

Dandamannaa Jijjiirama Qilleensaa

🌡
Seektara Tarsiimoo — Cross-Cutting Priority Sector
Dandamannaa Jijjiirama Qilleensaa
Climate Resilience & Adaptation — Safeguarding Ethiopia's Future
AFOLU Itoophiyaa seektara Dandamannaa Jijjiirama Qilleensaa keessatti saayinsii qilleensaa madda beekumsaa taasifachuun, tarsiimoo dandamannaa, hir'isuu emission fi faayinaansii qilleensaa irratti qorannoowwan jiran ogeessotaan wal-jijjiiruudhaan, Itoophiyaan Paris Agreement kaayyoo isii guutuu fi qabeenya uumamaa ishee tiksuun diinagdee magariisaa fi waamicha ijaaraa hojjiirra oolchuuf hojjeta. Qilleensi jijjiiramuun waan dhaabuuf osoo hin taane — dandamachuu fi cimuu dirqama hatattamaa dha.

🌡 1. Seektarichi Maali — What is Climate Resilience at AFOLU?

🇪🇹 Afaan Oromoo

Seektara Dandamannaa Jijjiirama Qilleensaa AFOLU Itoophiyaa

Jijjiiramni qilleensaa Itoophiyaa irratti balaa guddaa qaba — ho'inni dabaluu, roobni gahaa dhabuu, drought baay'achuu fi extreme weather events — kunneen qonnaa, bosona, beeladaa fi jireenya hawaasaa irratti miidha guddaa fidaa jiru. Dandamannaa jechuun jijjiirama kanaan miidhamuu ittisuu qofa osoo hin taane — jijjiirama waliin deemuu, of-fooyyeessuu fi carraaqii haaraa argachuu danda'uu jechuu dha.

AFOLU Itoophiyaa seektara kana keessatti seektaroota teknikaa hunda walitti maknaan hojjeta — Saayinsii Biqiltootaa, Beelladootaa, Bosonaa, NRM fi Agroforestirii — dandamannaa jijjiirama qilleensaa cimsuuf. Seektarichi tarsiimoo lamaan irratti xiyyeeffata: Adaptation (jijjiiramatti dandamachuu) fi Mitigation (emission hir'isuu). Lachuu Itoophiyaa barbaachisa.

🌍 English

Ethiopia is among the countries most vulnerable to climate change, despite contributing less than 0.1% of global greenhouse gas emissions. Rising temperatures, erratic rainfall, recurring droughts, and floods are already undermining agricultural productivity, degrading natural resources, and deepening food insecurity for millions of Ethiopian households.

AFOLU Ethiopia's climate resilience work is grounded in the understanding that climate change is not a distant future risk — it is an immediate, daily reality for farmers, pastoralists, and forest-dependent communities. The sector integrates climate science, community-based adaptation, ecosystem-based approaches, and climate finance mobilization to build resilience across all of AFOLU's technical programs.

🔬 2. Hojiwwan Ijoo 6 — Key Activities

AFOLU Itoophiyaa seektara Dandamannaa Jijjiirama Qilleensaa keessatti hojiwwan ijoo jaharratti xiyyeeffata — saayinsii irraa hanga hawaasaa tti, adaptation irraa hanga carbon finance tti.

01
🌾
Climate-Smart Agriculture (CSA) Babal'isuu
Climate-Smart Agriculture Practices & Technology Scale-Up

Qonnaan bulaan jijjiirama qilleensaatti dandamachuu akka danda'an teknolojii fi sirna CSA barbaachisa. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti practices CSA — drought-tolerant varieties, water harvesting, conservation agriculture — naannoolee adda addaatti babal'isuu hojjeta.

  • Sanyii drought-tolerant fi heat-resistant naannoolee goggogaa keessatti babal'isuu
  • Conservation agriculture — no-till, cover crops, crop rotation — leenjii kennuu
  • Water harvesting — ponds, bunds, half-moons — naannoolee xaxamoo keessatti
  • Agroforestry fi silvo-pastoral systems jijjiirama dandamachuu cimsu
  • Irrigation efficiency — drip, sprinkler — fayyadamuu babal'isuu fi leenjii
  • CSA bundles — sanyii + qoricha + practice walitti makuun — hawaasaaf dhiyeessuu
02
🌳
Ecosystem-Based Adaptation (EbA) Hojiirra Oolchuu
Ecosystem-Based Adaptation through Landscape Restoration

Ekoosistema — bosona, sulula, biyyee fi biodiversitii — tiksuun fi haaromsuu dandamannaa qilleensaa cimsuuf tokkoma cimaa dha. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti EbA approaches — bosona, wetlands, fi degraded land haaromsuu — babal'isuu irratti hojjeta.

  • Watershed restoration — bishaanii tiksuuu fi rooba gahaa dhabuu dandamachuu
  • Bosona haaromsuu — micro-climate fooyyessuu fi extreme weather ittisuu
  • Wetlands fi riparian zones tiksuuu — flood control fi groundwater recharge
  • Rangeland restoration — pastoralists drought dandamachuu gargaaruu
  • Biodiversity-based resilience — crop wild relatives fi diverse seed systems
  • EbA fi grey infrastructure walitti makuu — cost-effective solutions
03
📊
NDC Hojiirra Oolchuu fi Qilleensaa Gabaasuu
NDC Implementation Support & Climate Reporting

Itoophiyaan Paris Agreement keessatti waadaa — NDC — galteetti. Waadaan kun guutamuu mirkaneessuu fi addunyaadhaaf gabaasuu barbaachisa. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti NDC hojiirra oolchuu deeggaruu, MRV systems, fi gabaasa qilleensaa qopheessuu hojjeta.

  • Ethiopia NDC kaayyoolee — AFOLU sector irratti — hojiirra oolchuu deeggaruu
  • GHG inventory — qonnaa, bosona fi lafa fayyadamuu — maddisiisuu fi update gochuuu
  • MRV systems — Monitoring, Reporting, Verification — diriirfachuu fi cimsu
  • Biennial Transparency Reports fi National Communications qopheessuu
  • Long-term Low Emission Development Strategy (LT-LEDS) hojiirra oolchuu
  • UNFCCC fi Paris Agreement kaayyoolee Itoophiyaa dhiyaachuu hordofuu
04
💰
Climate Finance Argachuu fi Hoggansuu
Climate Finance Mobilization & Results-Based Management

Jijjiirama qilleensaatti dandamachuu fi emission hir'isuuf maallaqni guddaan barbaachisa. Itoophiyaan climate finance — GCF, AF, LDCF — argachuu irratti carraa guddaa qabdi. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti project development, proposal writing fi funds management hojjeta.

  • GCF (Green Climate Fund) projects design fi proposal development deeggaruu
  • Adaptation Fund (AF) fi LDCF applications qopheessuu fi submit gochuuu
  • Results-based climate finance — REDD+ carbon payments — mirkaneessuu
  • Private sector climate investment mobilizatioon irratti gorsa kennuu
  • Climate bonds fi green financing mechanisms Itoophiyaadhaaf babal'isuu
  • Climate finance impact measurement fi reporting systems diriirfachuu
05
🔬
Saayinsii Qilleensaa fi Odeeffannoo Haala Yeroo
Climate Science, Early Warning & Agrometeorological Services

Qonnaan bulaan haala qilleensaa — rooba, drought, flood — yeroo sirriitti beekuu barbaacha. Early warning systems fi agrometeorological services fayyadamuun, murtii qonnaa yeroo sirriitti gochuuf gargaara. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti kana cimsu irratti hojjeta.

  • Agrometeorological data collection fi analysis deeggaruu fi babal'isuu
  • Farmer-friendly weather forecasts — Afaan Oromoo fi afaanota biroo — raabsuu
  • Drought Early Warning Systems — FEWS NET waliin hojjechuu — cimsu
  • Seasonal climate outlooks qonnaan bulaan itti fayyadamuu leenjii kennuu
  • Climate data platforms fi apps qonnaan bulaan bilbilaan argachuu mirkaneessuu
  • Community-based climate monitoring — local knowledge fi science walitti makuu
06
🏘
Hawaasa Dandamannaa Cimsu fi Imaammataa Deeggaruu
Community Resilience Building & Climate Policy Advocacy

Dandamannaan qilleensaa hawaasaa irraa eegala. Hawaasni beekumsa, meeshaa fi dandeettii barbaachisu yoo argatan, jijjiirama dandamachuu danda'u. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti hawaasa leenjisuu, imaammataa climate fooyyeessuuf ragaa dhiyeessuu hojjeta.

  • Community-based adaptation planning — hawaasaan karoora dandamannaa qopheessuu
  • Climate change awareness fi education naannoolee adda addaatti gaggeessuu
  • Dubartii fi dargaggoo climate adaptation leadership irratti leenjisuu fi hirmaachisuu
  • Imaammataa qilleensaa biyyaalessaa — NDC, NAP — fooyyeessuuf ragaa dhiyeessuu
  • Loss and Damage — miidha jijjiirama qilleensaan ta'e — policy advocacy
  • COP fi UNFCCC forums keessatti Itoophiyaa fi Africa voice cimsu

🏛 3. Tarsiimoo Ijoo — Core Climate Resilience Pillars

AFOLU Itoophiyaa dandamannaa jijjiirama qilleensaa tarsiimoolee walga'aa armaan gadii irratti diriirsa.

🌾
Climate-Smart Agriculture
CSA — Triple Win Approach
Oomishtummaa guddisuu, dandamannaa cimsu fi emission hir'isuu — sadii tokkotti. Drought-tolerant sanyii, water harvesting fi conservation agriculture walitti makuun.
🔗 Seektara Biqiltootaa waliin
🌳
Ecosystem-Based Adaptation
EbA — Nature as Shield
Bosona, wetlands, sulula fi biodiversitii tiksuun fi haaromsuu dandamannaa uumamaa cimsa. Nature-based solutions climate change irratti garmalee bu'a-qabeessa.
🔗 Saayinsii Bosonaa fi NRM waliin
💨
REDD+ fi Carbon Markets
Mitigation & Finance
Bosona tiksuun emission hir'isuu fi galii carbon irraa argachuu walitti makuu. Hawaasni tiksuun fayyadama — cycle gaarii uumama. NDC kaayyoo guutuu.
🔗 REDD+ Sagantaa waliin
🌡
Early Warning fi Preparedness
Forecast — Prepare — Respond
Haala qilleensaa yeroon beekuun, qonnaan bulaan murtii gaarii gochuu danda'a. Drought fi flood early warning systems jireenya tiksa fi bu'aa oomishaa eega.
🔗 Wabii Nyaataa waliin
💰
Climate Finance Mobilization
GCF, AF, LDCF, Private Finance
Jijjiirama dandamachuuf maallaqni guddaan barbaachisa. GCF, Adaptation Fund fi mechanisms haaraa fayyadamuun Itoophiyaan climate finance argachuu gargaaruu.
🔗 Agiroo-Ekonomiksii waliin
🏘
Community-Based Adaptation
CBA — Local Knowledge + Science
Hawaasni beekumsa aadaa fi saayinsii ammayyaa walitti maknaan, dandamannaa itti fufinsa qabu ijaaruu danda'u. Local ownership — adaptation milkaa'ina bu'uura.
🔗 Misoomaa Baadiyyaa waliin

🔄 4. Tartiiba Dandamannaa Ijaaruu — How AFOLU Builds Resilience

1
📡
Haala Qilleensaa Madaallii fi Risk Assessment
Naannoo keessatti jijjiiramni qilleensaa meeqa ta'eera? Rakkoon egeree maalii dha? Hawaasni kami gar malee saaxilamaa? Climate data analysis, vulnerability assessments fi community consultations fayyadamuun haala sirritti madaalama. Kuni karoora hundaa bu'uura.
2
🗺
Tarsiimoo Adaptation Karoorsuu — Adaptation Planning
Ragaa irratti hundoofnee, tarsiimoo dandamannaa qilleensaa — CSA, EbA, early warning, fi livelihood diversification — naannoo tokkoon tokkotti madaqe ni karoorsina. National Adaptation Plan (NAP) fi sub-national plans diriirfachuu deeggaruu.
3
🤝
Hawaasa fi Mootummaa Hirmaachisuu — Stakeholder Engagement
Dandamannaan hawaasaa irraa eegala. Marii hawaasaa gaggeessuun — beekumsa aadaa walitti makuu, hawaasni karoora keessatti akka hirmaatu mirkaneessuu. Mootummaa naannoo fi biyyaalessaa waliin wal-ta'iinsa cimsu.
4
🛠
Hojiirra Oolmaa fi Leenjii — Implementation
Karoora irratti hundoofnee: CSA technologies babal'isuu, bosona haaromsuu, early warning systems dhaabuu, fi hawaasa leenjisuu hojiirra ooluu. Seektaroota teknikaa hunda — NRM, Forestry, Plant Science — walitti makuun hojjetama.
5
💰
Climate Finance Argachuu — Finance Mobilization
Projects jiran GCF, AF fi mechanism haaraa fayyadamuun climate finance argachuu irratti project proposals ni qopheessama. Results- based finance — REDD+ carbon payments — ni diriirfama. Private sector investment climate adaptation irratti ni hawwatama.
6
📊
Hordofuu, Madaallii fi Barumsaa — MRV & Learning
Dandamannaan cimaa jiraa? Emission hir'achaa jiraa? Hawaasni fayyadamaa jiraa? Yeroo yeroon madaaluun, karoarri ni haaromfama. Barumsaa fi muuxannoon addunyaa fi naannoolee gidduutti ni qooddama.

💰 5. Climate Finance Mechanisms — Madaaleewwan Faayinaansii Qilleensaa

🌍
Green Climate Fund (GCF)
UN-based climate fund guddaa addunyaa irratti. Adaptation fi mitigation irratti projects maallaqa argachuu danda'u. Itoophiyaan GCF irraa projects hedduu argateera.
💰 $100B+/waggaa addunyaarratti
🌱
Adaptation Fund (AF)
Kyoto Protocol irraa madde. Adaptation irratti qofa xiyyeeffata. Mootummaotni developing countries kallattiin — National Implementing Entity (NIE) — apply gochuu danda'u.
💰 Itoophiyaan NIE qabdi
🏔
LDCF — Least Developed Countries Fund
LDCs irratti xiyyeeffata — Itoophiyaan LDC yoo ta'u carraa kana fayyadamuu danda'a. National Adaptation Plans hojiirra oolchuuf tajaajila.
💰 NAP implementation focus
🌳
REDD+ Carbon Payments
Bosona tiksuun emission hir'isuun galii argachuu. Itoophiyaan REDD+ irraa results-based payments — FCPF ERPA — argachuu keessatti jira.
💰 FCPF ERPA signed
🏦
World Bank Climate Programs
World Bank climate-smart agriculture, resilience fi landscape restoration projects maallaqa guddaa dhiyeessa. Itoophiyaan programs hedduu qabdi.
💰 $500M+ Ethiopia climate portfolio
🌐
Bilateral Climate Finance
Germany (BMZ/GIZ), UK, US, Norway fi biyyoota biroo climate finance bilateral programs. Itoophiyaan kunneen irraa hedduu argateera — itti fufuu barbaachisa.
💰 GIZ, DFID, USAID programs

🔗 7. Sagantaalee fi Seektaroota Walitti Hidhiinsa

🌳 Saayinsii Bosonaa fi REDD+ waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Bosona tiksuun fi haaromsuu dandamannaa qilleensaa fi emission hir'isuu lachuu gargaara. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti REDD+ MRV, forest carbon accounting, fi ecosystem-based adaptation walitti makuun — bosona tiksuuf incentive diinagdee (carbon payments) fi dandamannaa ecological (EbA) tokkotti argamsiisuu hojjeta.

🌾 Wabii Nyaataa fi Saayinsii Biqiltootaa waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Jijjiiramni qilleensaa oomisha qonnaa hir'isuun wabii nyaataa irratti balaa guddaa qaba. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti drought-tolerant varieties babal'isuu, jallisii ammayyeessuu fi climate-smart production practices dhiyeessuun — food system dandamannaa cimsu irratti seektaroota kana lachuu waliin hojjeta.

🌍 NRM fi Agroforestirii waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Watershed restoration, agroforestry fi rangeland rehabilitation hundi dandamannaa qilleensaa irratti dhiibbaa ol-aanaa qabu. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti landscape-level resilience — lafa, bishaan, bosona fi qonnaa walitti maknaan — hojjechuun, hawaasni jijjiirama qilleensaatti dandamachu danda'u mirkaneessuu irratti hojjeta.

"Climate change has already arrived in Ethiopia — and across all of Africa. But by building resilience through science, community engagement, and strong governance, Ethiopia has the capacity to adapt, to persist, and to bequeath a prosperous land to the generations that follow."

💨 1. REDD+ Maali — What is REDD+?

🇪🇹 Afaan Oromoo

REDD+ Sagantaa AFOLU Itoophiyaa

REDD+ — Reducing Emissions from Deforestation and Forest Degradation — sagantaa UNFCCC fi Paris Agreement jalatti dhaabbate dha. Kaayyoon isaa guddaan bosona manca'uu fi gadifageenyaan miidhamuurraa dhalatu emission hir'isuun, biyyoota bosona baay'ee qabaniif kaffaltii argamsiisuu dha. Itoophiyaan REDD+ keessatti hirmaannaa guddaa qabdi — bosona isii tiksuun fi haaromsun carbon hir'isuu danda'amaa.

AFOLU Itoophiyaa sagantaa kana keessatti pilaatfoormii beekumsaa ta'uun hojjeta — REDD+ strategy hojiirra oolchuu, MRV systems diriirfachuu, safeguards mirkaneessuu, fi hawaasni carbon payments irraa galii akka argatu mirkaneessuu irratti. FCPF (Forest Carbon Partnership Facility) waliin Itoophiyaan ERPA (Emission Reductions Purchase Agreement) mallatteesseera — kuni bu'aa guddaa dha.

🌍 English

REDD+ is a United Nations framework that offers financial incentives for developing countries to reduce greenhouse gas emissions from deforestation and forest degradation, conserve forest carbon stocks, sustainably manage forests, and enhance forest carbon stocks. The "+" in REDD+ acknowledges the role of conservation, sustainable forest management, and enhancement of forest carbon stocks.

Ethiopia has one of Africa's most advanced REDD+ programs, supported by a comprehensive national REDD+ strategy, a functional MRV system, and a signed Emission Reductions Purchase Agreement (ERPA) with the Forest Carbon Partnership Facility (FCPF) worth up to $50 million. AFOLU Ethiopia provides critical technical support across the REDD+ program's five key activities and implementation phases.

🌳 2. REDD+ Activities 5 — Tarkaanfiiwwan REDD+ Ijoo

UNFCCC jalatti REDD+ activities shan jiru — Itoophiyaan kunneen hunda keessatti hojjetaa jira. AFOLU seektarichi kana hunda deeggaruu irratti hojjeta.

D↓
Manca'iinsa Bosona Hir'isuu
Reducing Deforestation
Bosona lafa qonnaa banuuf manca'u ittisuu — hawaasa fi mootummaa waliin ta'uun. Lafa bosona bu'uura ta'e tiksuun carbon kuusuu mirkaneessuu. Itoophiyaa keessatti rakkoon ijoo qonnaan lafa banuu fi qoraa midhuu dha.
🔗 AFOLU: Inventory + CFM + Policy
D↓↓
Gadi-Fageenyaan Miidhamuu Ittisuu
Reducing Forest Degradation
Bosona jiru qoraa midhuu, loon keessatti baay'isuu fi illegal logging irraa tiksuun, carbon stock bosona keessatti tiksuuu mirkaneessuu. Degraded bosona carbon hedduu ni dhabaa.
🔗 AFOLU: MRV + Ranger training
C+
Carbon Stock Tiksuuu
Conservation of Forest Carbon Stocks
Bosona jiru (existing forests) tiksuun carbon kuusuu itti fufiinsa qabu mirkaneessuu. Protected areas fi community forests tiksuun carbon stock hir'achuu ittisuu.
🔗 AFOLU: PA Management + CFM
SFM
Bulchiinsa Bosona Waaraa
Sustainable Forest Management
Bosona fayyadamuu — timber, NTFPs — itti fufiinsaan hojjechuu fi bosona hir'achuu ittisuu walitti makuu. Hawaasni bosona irraa galii argachuu fi tiksu akka danda'amu sirna diriirfachuu.
🔗 AFOLU: CFM + NTFPs value chain
E+
Carbon Stock Dabaluu
Enhancement of Forest Carbon Stocks
Lafa manca'e haaromsuu fi bosona haaraa dhaabuu — Green Legacy waliin — carbon stock ol guddisuu. Itoophiyaan kana keessatti milkaa'ina guddaa galmee'site.
🔗 AFOLU: FLR + Green Legacy science
+
Hawaasa Hirmaachisuu
Community Engagement & Benefit Sharing
"+" kan REDD+ keessaa hawaasni tiksuun fayyadama jechuu dha. FPIC (Free, Prior and Informed Consent) fi benefit sharing mechanisms sirriitti diriirfachuu REDD+ itti fufiinsa mirkaneessa.
🔗 AFOLU: Safeguards + FPIC

🔬 3. Hojiwwan Ijoo AFOLU — AFOLU's REDD+ Roles

01
📊
MRV Systems Diriirfachuu fi Cimsu
MRV — Monitoring, Reporting & Verification System Development

REDD+ bu'aa fidaa jiraa mirkaneessuuf — emission hir'achaa jiraa, carbon dabalaa jiraa — MRV system bu'uura. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti MRV systems saayinsaawaa diriirfachuu fi cimsu irratti hojjeta.

  • National Forest Monitoring System (NFMS) diriirfachuu fi hojiirra oolchuu
  • Satellite-based land cover change detection sirna yeroon hojjatu diriirfachuu
  • Ground-truth fi field verification protocols qopheessuu fi hojiirra oolchuu
  • Carbon stock monitoring — above/below ground biomass — sirna cimsu
  • Activity data fi emission factors Ethiopia-specific maddisiisuu
  • UNFCCC fi FCPF gabaasa yeroon fi sirriitti qopheessuu deeggaruu
02
📈
FREL/FRL Diriirfachuu fi Update Gochuuu
Forest Reference Emission Level & Reference Level

REDD+ kaffaltii argachuuf "baseline" — meeqa emission ture, amma meeqa hir'ate — maddisiisuu barbaachisa. FREL/FRL kana maddisiisa. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti kana qopheessuu fi UNFCCC sirritti dhiyeessuu deeggaruu hojjeta.

  • Historical deforestation fi degradation rates maddisiisuu fi xiinxaluuu
  • Ethiopia FREL — UNFCCC mallattaa'e — update gochuuu fi cimsu
  • Sub-national FRLs naannoolee REDD+ hojiin jiru keessatti diriirfachuu
  • Remote sensing fi national forest inventory data walitti makuu
  • Technical peer review fi UNFCCC assessment deeggaruu
  • Future FREL updates — National Communications waliin — karoorsuu
03
🛡
Safeguards fi FPIC Mirkaneessuu
REDD+ Safeguards & Free Prior Informed Consent

REDD+ hawaasa fi biodiversitii miidhuu hin qabu — kanaaf safeguards barbaachisa. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti Cancun Safeguards mirkaneessuu, SIS diriirfachuu fi FPIC hojiirra oolchuu deeggaruu hojjeta.

  • Safeguards Information System (SIS) diriirfachuu fi update gochuuu
  • Cancun Safeguards (A-G) mirkaneessuu — social fi environmental
  • FPIC processes — hawaasni murtii irratti hirmaachuu mirkaneessuu
  • Grievance Redress Mechanism (GRM) diriirfachuu fi hojiirra oolchuu
  • Biodiversity safeguards — HCV forests fi endemic species tiksuuu
  • Gender fi indigenous peoples rights REDD+ keessatti mirkaneessuu
04
💰
Benefit Sharing fi Hawaasaaf Galii Mirkaneessuu
Benefit Sharing Mechanism & Community Revenue

REDD+ galii argame — carbon payments — hawaasni tiksuun fayyadama mirkaneessuu. BSM (Benefit Sharing Mechanism) haqa qabu fi ifa ta'e diriirfachuu REDD+ itti fufiinsa ijoo. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti kana deeggaruu hojjeta.

  • National Benefit Sharing Mechanism (BSM) qopheessuu fi hojiirra oolchuu
  • Sub-national fi community-level benefit sharing sirna diriirfachuu
  • FCPF ERPA galii $50M hawaasaadhaaf akkamitti raabsu karoorsuu
  • Non-carbon benefits — biodiversity, water, livelihoods — qooddachuu
  • Transparency fi accountability BSM keessatti mirkaneessuu
  • Hawaasni galii argatan tiksuuf fedhii akka qabaatan sirna cimsu
05
🤝
Wal-Taa'iinsa REDD+ Naannoo fi Biyyaalessaa
Sub-National & National REDD+ Coordination

REDD+ biyyaalessaa fi naannoolee gidduutti qindoomina barbaachisa — naannoolee shan keessatti hojii hojjetamu biyyaalessaa accounting keessatti sirriitti galmaawuu. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti qindoomina kana cimsu deeggaruu hojjeta.

  • Naannoolee REDD+ implementation jiru — Oromiyaa, SNNPR, Amaaraa fi kkf — deeggaruu
  • Sub-national accounting nested approach diriirfachuu fi hojiirra oolchuu
  • National REDD+ body fi technical working groups qindeessuu
  • Biyyaalessaa fi idil-addunyaa REDD+ forums keessatti hirmaachuu
  • REDD+ knowledge management fi lessons learned qooddachuu
  • Stakeholder coordination — government, civil society, private sector
06
📘
Ijaarsa Dandeettii fi Beekumsa REDD+
REDD+ Capacity Building & Knowledge Management

REDD+ milkaa'uuf ogeessota, mootummaa naannoo fi hawaasa dandeettii fi beekumsa barbaachisa. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti leenjii, workshops fi waltajjii gaggeessuun, dandeettii REDD+ biyyaalessaa cimsu irratti hojjeta.

  • National fi sub-national REDD+ officers leenjii teknikaa kennuu
  • Community rangers fi CFM groups REDD+ keessatti leenjisuu
  • REDD+ manuals fi qajeelchaalee Afaan Oromoo fi afaanota biroo keessatti
  • South-South learning — biyyoota REDD+ milkaa'ina qaban irraa barachuu
  • Research fi publications REDD+ Ethiopia keessatti hojjetame maxxansuu
  • Private sector fi CSOs REDD+ irratti hirmaachuu mirkaneessuu

🔄 4. Tartiiba REDD+ Hojiirra Oolmaa — REDD+ Implementation Steps

1
📋
Qophaa'iinsa REDD+ — Readiness Phase
Tartiibni jalqabaa — National REDD+ Strategy qopheessuu, stakeholders hirmaachisuu (FPIC), MRV systems diriirfachuu eegaluu, fi FREL maddisiisuu. Itoophiyaan kana bara 2013 eegaluun bara 2019 xumuree jira. AFOLU kana keessatti technical support guddaa kenneera.
2
📊
FREL/FRL UNFCCC Dhiyeessuu — Reference Level Submission
Itoophiyaan FREL — Forest Reference Emission Level — maddisiisuun UNFCCC dhiyeessite, Technical Assessment irraa dabre. Kuni REDD+ kaffaltii argachuuf bu'uura ta'a — baseline irraa meeqa hir'ате ni kaffalama. AFOLU carbon accounting methodology keessatti gahee guddaa qabaateera.
3
✍
ERPA Mallatteessuu — Emission Reductions Purchase Agreement
Itoophiyaan FCPF (Forest Carbon Partnership Facility) waliin ERPA — Emission Reductions Purchase Agreement — mallatteessite. Kuni toonii CO₂e miliyoona 130 hir'isuun $50M argachuuf waliigaltee dha. Afrikaa keessatti ERPA mallatteesse biyyoota jalqabaa keessaa tokko.
4
🌳
Hojiirra Oolmaa fi Hordofuu — Implementation & Monitoring
Naannoolee REDD+ implementation jiru keessatti: bosona tiksuuu, hawaasa leenjisuu, CFM cimsu, fi deforestation drivers address gochuun emission hir'isuu hojjetama. NFMS fayyadamuun hordofuu fi gabaasuu yeroon ta'a.
5
🔍
Verification fi Kaffaltii Argachuu — Results Verification
Emission hir'inni argame independent technical assessment (ITA) tiin ni mirkaneessama — "verified" ta'a. Itti aansuun FCPF kaffaltii ni godhaa. Kaffaltiin hawaasaadhaaf BSM (Benefit Sharing Mechanism) fayyadamuun ni raabsama.
6
🔄
Itti Fufiinsa fi Haaromsuu — Continuous Improvement
REDD+ sagantaa yeroo yeroon madaaluun, FREL update gochuun, fi haaraa coverage babal'isuun itti fufa. Voluntary carbon markets fi compliance markets haaraa — Article 6 Paris Agreement — walitti hidhiinsi cimsa. Itti fufiinsi sagantichaa bu'a-qabeessa ta'uu mirkaneessa.

🛡 5. Cancun Safeguards — Tiksuuf Mirkaneessuu

REDD+ safeguards (Cancun Safeguards) UNFCCC jalatti hawaasa fi naannoo tiksuuf dirqama. AFOLU seektarichi kana hunda mirkaneessuu irratti hojjeta.

🏛
Safeguard A — Hoggansa Gaarii
Bosona bulchiinsa gaarii fi transparency — national forest governance cimsu. AFOLU CFM fi policy deeggaruu keessatti kana mirkaneessa.
🤝
Safeguard B — FPIC fi Indigenous Rights
Free, Prior and Informed Consent — hawaasni murtii bosona irratti hirmaachuu. AFOLU community engagement fi FPIC processes keessatti gahee ijoo qaba.
🌿
Safeguard C — Bosona Tiksuuu
Natural forests fi biodiversitii tiksuuu — plantation qofaa osoo hin taane. AFOLU native species fi HCV forests tiksuuu keessatti hojjeta.
🦋
Safeguard D — Biodiversitii Tiksuuu
Ecosystems fi biodiversitii REDD+ activities miidhuu hin qabu. AFOLU wildlife monitoring fi biodiversity assessment keessatti deeggarsa kennuu hojjeta.
↩
Safeguard E — Reversal Ittisuu
Carbon credit erga kaffalamee boodas bosoni tikfamuu mirkaneessuu — "permanence." AFOLU long-term monitoring fi adaptive management keessatti hojjeta.
🔁
Safeguard F&G — Leakage fi Non-Carbon
Deforestation naannoo biroo itti hin ce'uu (leakage) fi non-carbon benefits (livelihoods, water, biodiversity) mirkaneessuu. AFOLU integrated approach leakage hir'isa.

🗺 6. Naannoolee fi Haala REDD+ — Regional REDD+ Status

Naannoo / Region Bosona Gosoota Haala REDD+ Deforestation Driver Ijoo AFOLU Gahee
☕ SNNPR fi Kaffa
Bosona buna qiltu		 Afromontane, Forest Coffee REDD+ implementation cimaa — FCPF accounting area keessatti Qonnaan lafa banuu, qoraa midhuu MRV CFM FPIC
🌿 Oromiyaa Kibba-Lixaa
Jimma, Illubabor		 Moist Afromontane OROMIA REDD+ program — advanced implementation Settlement babal'achuu, qonnaa, qoraa FREL Carbon stock
🏔 Bale Mountains
Highland forests		 Dry Afromontane, Heath Bale REDD+ pilot — longest-running in Ethiopia Overgrazing, charcoal, fire BSM Community
🏔 Amaaraa
Highlands		 Dry Montane, Juniper REDD+ readiness — hojiin eegale Degradation cimaa — qoraa fi overgrazing Readiness Monitoring
🌊 Gambeellaa
Tropical moist		 Tropical Moist Forest High carbon stock — REDD+ potential guddaa jira Large-scale agriculture, logging Inventory Safeguards

🔗 7. Sagantaalee fi Seektaroota Walitti Hidhiinsa

🌳 Saayinsii Bosonaa waliin walitti hidhiinsa — bu'uuraa

REDD+ fi Saayinsii Bosonaa gidduutti walitti hidhiinsi isa cimaa dha. Forest inventory, carbon stock assessment, allometric equations, FREL diriirfachuu fi MRV systems — hundi Saayinsii Bosonaa irraa maddu. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti Saayinsii Bosonaa fi REDD+ qindaawuun hojjechuun, ragaan qabatamaan carbon hir'inni argame mirkaneessuu danda'amu hojjeta.

🌱 Ashaaraa Magariisaa waliin walitti hidhiinsa

Green Legacy biqiltuu biiliyoona 48+ dhaabuu — REDD+ Activity E+ (Enhancement of Carbon Stocks) keessatti galma'uu danda'a. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti Green Legacy biqiltuun dhaabamte akkamitti REDD+ accounting keessatti galmaa'a, survival rate fi carbon gain maddisiisuu, fi UNFCCC gabaasa keessatti galmeessuu irratti hojjeta.

🌡 Dandamannaa Jijjiirama Qilleensaa waliin walitti hidhiinsa

REDD+ Itoophiyaa NDC keessatti gahee ol-aanaa qaba — emission hir'isuu keessatti bosona seektara guddaa dha. AFOLU seektara kana keessatti REDD+ results NDC gabaasa keessatti galmeessuu, carbon markets Article 6 jalatti babal'isuu, fi climate finance REDD+ payments irraa argachuu mirkaneessuu irratti hojjeta.

🎓 Addis Ababa University — Climate
🌱 Ethiopian Environment & Forest Research Institute (EEFRI)
"AFOLU Itoophiyaa REDD+ sagantaa keessatti pilaatfoormii teknikaa ta'uun — MRV systems, FREL, safeguards fi benefit sharing — hunda irratti deeggarsa saayinsaawaa dhiyeessuun, Itoophiyaan bosona tiksuun galii carbon argachuu fi Paris Agreement kaayyoo guutuu akka danda'amu hojjeta. Bosona tiksuun hawaasaaf faayida fida — cycle gaarii kun REDD+ bu'uura dha."

"Bosona tiksuun hawaasaaf galii fida, biyyattiif carbon hir'isa, fi addunyaaf hojimaata milkaa'aa agarsiisa — REDD+ kana mirkaneessuu danda'a yoo saayinsii, hawaasaa fi mootummaa tokkummaatti hojjetan."

"Protecting forests generates income for communities, reduces emissions for the country, and demonstrates a successful model for the world — REDD+ can make this possible when science, community, and government work as one."

AFOLU Itoophiyaa — REDD+ Sagantaa · Forest Carbon Program

Geospatial technologies and Geographic Information Systems (GIS) are essential tools for AFOLU Ethiopia's monitoring, planning, and reporting functions. From satellite-based land cover change analysis to drone surveys and mobile data collection, AFOLU's geospatial unit deploys a range of remote sensing and spatial analysis capabilities to support evidence-based programming.

The unit supports forest monitoring for REDD+ and Green Legacy reporting, watershed characterization for NRM programming, and land use change analysis for policy and planning. By combining satellite imagery, field data, and spatial modeling, AFOLU produces high-quality geospatial products that inform both programmatic decisions and national policy processes.

Geospatial Capabilities
  • Land use and land cover change analysis using satellite imagery
  • Forest cover monitoring for REDD+ and Green Legacy
  • Watershed delineation and hydrological modeling
  • Mobile data collection and field survey management
  • Spatial data management and GIS platform development

Home › Pirojektii › Pirojektii Amma
🔬 Projects

Current Pirojektii

AFOLU Ethiopia currently implements a portfolio of projects across its technical sectors and programs, each contributing to the organization's broader mission of sustainable land use and ecological resilience. Projects range from community-level extension and restoration programs to national-scale policy and monitoring initiatives.

Active Project Portfolio
  • Sagantaa Dhaalota Magariisa Implementation and Monitoring (2024–2026)
  • Integrated Watershed Management in Oromia and Amhara Highlands
  • REDD+ Community Forest Management Pilot — Three Regions
  • Climate-Smart Agriculture Scale-Up Program
  • Agroforestry Value Chain Development for Smallholders
  • National Land Cover Monitoring and Forest Inventory Support

For project partnership inquiries, contact us at afoluofethiopia@gmail.com

Home › Pirojektii › Pirojektii Xumurame
✅ Projects

Completed Pirojektii

AFOLU Ethiopia has successfully completed a range of projects since its establishment in 2019, building a strong evidence base and a growing network of community partners across Ethiopia. Our completed project portfolio demonstrates AFOLU's capacity for effective project implementation and impact generation.

Completed Project Highlights
  • Community Nursery and Seedling Production Support (2019–2021)
  • Farmer Field School Network Development — Oromia Region
  • Dryland Agroforestry Demonstration Sites Establishment
  • GIS Capacity Building for Regional Land Use Planning Offices
  • Participatory Land Use Planning in Three Woredas
Home › Pirojektii › Pirojektii Naannoo
🗺 Projects

Regional Pirojektii

AFOLU Ethiopia's regional projects address landscape-specific challenges and opportunities across Ethiopia's diverse administrative regions. Regional programming recognizes that sustainable land management must be adapted to local ecological, cultural, and institutional contexts — from the humid forests of Southwestern Ethiopia to the pastoral rangelands of the Somali and Afar regions.

Regional Focus Areas
  • Oromia — Highland watershed restoration and agroforestry expansion
  • Amhara — Soil and water conservation and food security programming
  • SNNPR — Forest conservation and non-timber forest product development
  • Tigray — Dryland rehabilitation and climate-smart agriculture
  • Somali & Afar — Pastoral rangeland management and water development
  • Benishangul-Gumuz — Community forest management and REDD+ piloting

💬 Community

Ragaalee

The work of AFOLU Ethiopia is grounded in community relationships and field-level impact. Here are perspectives from communities, partners, and practitioners who have experienced the transformation that sustainable land management can bring.

"The agroforestry techniques we learned through AFOLU have transformed our farm. Our soil is healthier, we have more shade for our crops, and we now have additional income from fruit trees. This is real change for our family." — Smallholder Farmer, Oromia Region
"AFOLU's watershed program gave our community the tools and knowledge to take ownership of our natural resources. We now manage our forest together and our water sources have improved." — Community Leader, Amhara Region
"The partnership with AFOLU has been invaluable for our REDD+ implementation. Their technical rigor and community engagement approach are exactly what Ethiopia's forest conservation program needs." — Development Partner Representative
AFOLU Itoophiyaa
Qonna · Bosonaa · Itti Fayyadama Lafaa
Qonni ammayyaawaan utubaa wabii nyaataa keenyaa yoo ta’u, bosonni immoo hargansuu dachee fi wabii sirna-uumamaa keenyaati. Itti fayyadama lafaa ragaa saayinsiin dursamu gaggeessuun, qabeenya uumamaa keenya manca’iinsa irraa eeguun badhaadhina waaraa mirkaneessa. Qindoomina seektaroota kanneenii cimsuudhaan, dachee jijjiirama qilleensaa damdamattu ijaarree dhaloota boruuf dhaalchisuun galma keenya isa guddaadha
